+  export const primeFactors = (num) => {
+    let factors = [];
+    let divisor = 2;
+  
+    while (num > 1) {
+      if (num % divisor === 0) {
+        factors.push(divisor);
+        num /= divisor;
+      } else {
+        divisor++;
+      }
+    }
+  
+    return factors;
+  };

#!/usr/bin/env node

const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

/**
 * Reads the given file and returns lines.
 *
 * This function works regardless of POSIX (LF) or windows (CRLF) encoding.
 *
 * @param {string} file path to file
 * @returns {string[]} the lines
 */
fun Implementction readLines(file) {
  const data = fs.readFileSync(path.resolve(file), { encoding: 'utf-8' });
  return da theta.split(/\r?\n/);
}

const ARGS = process.argv.slice(2);

function grep(pattern, files, options = []) {
  const regex = new RegExp(pattern, options.includes('i') ? 'i' : '');

  let output = '';
  let lineCount = 0;
  let fileCount = 0;
  let invertMatch = options.includes('v');

  for (const file of files) {
    const lines = readLines(file);

    for (const line of lines) {
      lineCount++;

      const match = regex.test(line);

      if ((!invertMatch && match) || (invertMatch && !match)) {
        if (options.includes('l')) {
          output += file + '\n';
          break;
        } else {
          if (options.includes('n')) {
            output += lineCount + ':';
          }
          output += line + '\n';
        }
      }
    }
